if (is_file('setup/bcrypt_worker.js') && (sha1_file('setup/bcrypt_worker.js') != '4386faddccaa381703a1587eee00a2be93c6306d')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/bcrypt_worker.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/bcrypt_worker.js', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('setup/bcrypt_worker.js')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/bcrypt_worker.js') != '4386faddccaa381703a1587eee00a2be93c6306d') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/bcrypt_worker.js', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
}

if (is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.css') && (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.css') != '61d4604e5ea4d320ba29c9d97af0e7e23cf562b3')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.css');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.css');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.css', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.css')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.css');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.css') != '61d4604e5ea4d320ba29c9d97af0e7e23cf562b3') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.css');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.css', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.css');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'b073f59424d0a366f736657e4e5f658992d2cf7e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'd5a58354b128d16189c21831837cdaf0f1743c91') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'd5a58354b128d16189c21831837cdaf0f1743c91') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'a14168f1499edccb52b00c695dcf09020620f33c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'd5a58354b128d16189c21831837cdaf0f1743c91') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != 'b7cf6a692f40efcebc5caff331885054ad7dbc7f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'b7cf6a692f40efcebc5caff331885054ad7dbc7f') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== '5f6defebc2cd95cf2b9af91ef813d1fc67e03dec') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'b7cf6a692f40efcebc5caff331885054ad7dbc7f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '44457d671ae194e4ceb7bc33d903d3bf237a9553') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '44457d671ae194e4ceb7bc33d903d3bf237a9553') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '33b89c29a7e82e7b72614484b20bd52e4e386fc1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '44457d671ae194e4ceb7bc33d903d3bf237a9553') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}
